Theravāda Vinayapiṭaka Theravāda Collection on Monastic Law

Cūḷavagga The Short Division

Samuccayakkhandhaka The chapter on accumulation in regard to the process for making amends for offenses entailing suspension

1. Sukkavissaṭṭhi Emission of semen

Tena samayena buddho bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati jetavane anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme. At one time the Buddha was staying at Sāvatthī in the Jeta Grove, Anāthapiṇḍika’s Monastery. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā udāyī ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpanno hoti sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. At that time Venerable Udāyī had committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks about this, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? adding, “What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should give the monk Udāyī the trial period of six days for one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbaṃ— And it should be given in this way:

1.1. Appaṭicchannamānatta Trial periods for those with unconcealed offenses

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā añjaliṃ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo— “The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. ‘Venerables, I have committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmi. I ask the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense.

Ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. I have committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Dutiyampi, sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmi. For the second time I ask the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense.

Ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. I have committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Tatiyampi sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmī’ti. For the third time I ask the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense.’

Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī has committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him the trial period of six days for that offense. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī has committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense. Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ deti. The Order gives him the trial period of six days for that offense. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him the trial period of six days for that offense should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi— For the second time I speak on this matter. suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī has committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense. Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ deti. The Order gives him the trial period of six days for that offense. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him the trial period of six days for that offense should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi— For the third time I speak on this matter. suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī has committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense. Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ deti. The Order gives him the trial period of six days for that offense. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him the trial period of six days for that offense should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dinnaṃ saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. The Order has given the monk Udāyī the trial period of six days for one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.2. Appaṭicchannaabbhāna Rehabilitation for those with unconcealed offenses

So ciṇṇamānatto bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— When he had completed the trial period, he told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. “I had committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense. Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. The Order gave me the trial period, Sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto. and I have now completed it. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbhetu. “Well then, the Order should rehabilitate the monk Udāyī. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, abbhetabbo— And it should be done in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā añjaliṃ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo— The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ, sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. ‘Venerables, I had committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. I asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me the trial period. Sohaṃ, bhante, ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācāmi. I have now completed the trial period and I ask the Order for rehabilitation.

Ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. I had committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me the trial period. Sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto dutiyampi, bhante, saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācāmi. I have now completed the trial period and for the second time I ask the Order for rehabilitation.

Ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. I had committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me the trial period. Sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto tatiyampi, bhante, saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācāmī’ti. I have now completed the trial period and for the third time I ask the Order for rehabilitation.’

Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him the trial period. So ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. He has now completed the trial period and is asking the Order for rehabilitation. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should rehabilitate him. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him the trial period. So ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. He has now completed the trial period and is asking the Order for rehabilitation. Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheti. The Order rehabilitates him. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno abbhānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of rehabilitating him should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi— For the second time I speak on this matter. suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him the trial period. So ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. He has now completed the trial period and is asking the Order for rehabilitation. Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheti. The Order rehabilitates him. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno abbhānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of rehabilitating him should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi— For the third time I speak on this matter. suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him the trial period. So ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. He has now completed the trial period and is asking the Order for rehabilitation. Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheti. The Order rehabilitates him. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno abbhānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of rehabilitating him should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Abbhito saṃghena udāyī bhikkhu. The Order has rehabilitated the monk Udāyī. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.3. Ekāhappaṭicchannaparivāsa Probation for those with offenses concealed for one day

Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā udāyī ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpanno hoti sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. On one occasion Venerable Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks about this, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? adding, “What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should give the monk Udāyī probation for one day for one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo— And it should be given in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā añjaliṃ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo— The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. ‘Venerables, I have committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. I ask the Order for probation for one day for that offense.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbo. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbo. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for probation for one day for that offense. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him that probation. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for probation for one day for that offense. Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ deti. The Order gives him that probation. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him that probation should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Dinno saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāso. The Order has given the monk Udāyī probation for one day for one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.4. Ekāhappaṭicchannamānatta Trial periods for those with offenses concealed for one day

So parivutthaparivāso bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— When he had completed the probation, he told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for one day for that offense. Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. The Order gave me that probation, Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso. and I have now completed it. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should give the monk Udāyī the trial period of six days for one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbaṃ— And it should be given in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. ‘Venerables, I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for one day for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Sohaṃ, bhante, parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmī’ti. I have now completed that probation and I ask the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. and a third time.

Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for probation for one day for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. So parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. He has now completed that probation and is asking the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him the trial period of six days. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for probation for one day for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. So parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. He has now completed that probation and is asking the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense. Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ deti. The Order gives him the trial period of six days. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him the trial period of six days should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Dinnaṃ saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. The Order has given the monk Udāyī the trial period of six days for one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.5. Ekāhappaṭicchannaabbhāna Rehabilitation for those with offenses concealed for one day

So ciṇṇamānatto bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— When he had completed the trial period, he told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for one day for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. When I had completed the probation, I asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense. Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. The Order gave me the trial period, Sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto. and I have now completed it. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbhetu. “Well then, the Order should rehabilitate the monk Udāyī. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, abbhetabbo— And it should be done in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. ‘I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for one day for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. When I had completed the probation, I asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me the trial period. Sohaṃ, bhante, ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācāmī’ti. I have now completed the trial period and I ask the Order for rehabilitation.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. And he should ask for a second Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for probation for one day for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. So parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. When he had completed the probation, he asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him the trial period. So ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. He has now completed the trial period and is asking the Order for rehabilitation. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should rehabilitate him. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ ekāhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for one day. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for probation for one day for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya ekāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. So parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. When he had completed the probation, he asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā ekāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him the trial period. So ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. He has now completed the trial period and is asking the Order for rehabilitation. Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheti. The Order rehabilitates him. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno abbhānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of rehabilitating him should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Abbhito saṃghena udāyī bhikkhu. The Order has rehabilitated the monk Udāyī. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.6. Pañcāhappaṭicchannaparivāsa Probation for those with offenses concealed for five days

Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā udāyī ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpanno hoti sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ dvīhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … On one occasion Venerable Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for two days. … tīhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … concealed for three days. … catūhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … concealed for four days. … pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. concealed for five days. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks about this, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? adding, “What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should give the monk Udāyī probation for five days for one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo— And it should be given in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā añjaliṃ paggahetvā evamassa vacanīyo— The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. ‘Venerables, I have committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. I ask the Order for probation for five days for that offense.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbo. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbo. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for probation for five days for that offense. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him that probation. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for probation for five days for that offense. Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ deti. The Order gives him that probation. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him that probation should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Dinno saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāso. The Order has given the monk Udāyī probation for five days for one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.7. Pārivāsikamūlāyapaṭikassanā Sending back to the beginning for those on probation

So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While he was on probation, he committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for five days for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While on probation, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassatu. “Well then, the Order should send the monk Udāyī back to the beginning for one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen, committed while on probation. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo— And it should be done in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. ‘Venerables, I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for five days for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While on probation, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācāmī’ti. I ask the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbā. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbā. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for probation for five days for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While he was on probation, he committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. He is now asking the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikasseyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should send him back to the beginning. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for probation for five days for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While he was on probation, he committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. He is now asking the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense. Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassati. The Order sends him back to the beginning. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of sending him back to the beginning should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Paṭikassito saṃghena udāyī bhikkhu antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā. The Order has sent the monk Udāyī back to the beginning for one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen, committed while on probation. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.8. Mānattārahamūlāyapaṭikassanā Sending back to the beginning for those deserving the trial period

So parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. When he had completed the probation, while deserving the trial period, he committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for five days for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While on probation, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, Taṃ maṃ saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. and the Order sent me back to the beginning. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. When I had completed the probation, while deserving the trial period, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassatu. “Well then, the Order should send the monk Udāyī back to the beginning for one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen, committed while deserving the trial period. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo— And it should be done in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … ‘Venerables, I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. … sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. When I had completed the probation, while deserving the trial period, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācāmī’ti. I ask the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, committed while deserving the trial period.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbā. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbā. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. … so parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. When he had completed the probation, while deserving the trial period, he committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, committed while deserving the trial period. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikasseyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should send him back to the beginning. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. … so parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. When he had completed the probation, while deserving the trial period, he committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, committed while deserving the trial period. Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassati. The Order sends him back to the beginning. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of sending him back to the beginning should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Paṭikassito saṃghena udāyī bhikkhu antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā. The Order has sent the monk Udāyī back to the beginning for one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen, committed while deserving the trial period. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.9. Tikāpattimānatta Trial period for the three offenses

So parivutthaparivāso bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— When he had completed the probation, he told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days … sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso. I have now completed the probation. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should give the monk Udāyī the trial period of six days for the three offenses. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbaṃ— And it should be given in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. ‘Venerables, I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for five days for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi … pe … and the Order gave me that probation. … sohaṃ, bhante, parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmī’ti. I have now completed that probation and I ask the Order for the trial period of six days for the three offenses.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. … so parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. He has now completed that probation and is asking the Order for the trial period of six days for the three offenses. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him the trial period of six days for the three offenses. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. … so parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. He has now completed that probation and is asking the Order for the trial period of six days for the three offenses. Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ deti. The Order gives him the trial period of six days for the three offenses. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him the trial period of six days for the three offenses should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Dinnaṃ saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. The Order has given the monk Udāyī the trial period of six days for the three offenses. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.10. Mānattacārikamūlāyapaṭikassanā Sending back to the beginning of those undertaking the trial period

So mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While he was undertaking the trial period, he committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. … sohaṃ mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While undertaking the trial period, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassitvā chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should send the monk Udāyī back to the beginning for one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen, committed while undertaking the trial period. It should then give him the trial period of six days. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo— And he should be sent back to the beginning like this:

tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … ‘Venerables, I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. … sohaṃ mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While undertaking the trial period, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācāmī’ti. I ask the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, committed while undertaking the trial period.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbā. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbā. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu … pe … This monk Udāyī … mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. is asking the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, committed while undertaking the trial period. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikasseyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should send him back to the beginning. Esā ñatti … pe … This is the motion. … paṭikassito saṃghena udāyī bhikkhu antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā. The Order has sent the monk Udāyī back to the beginning for one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen, committed while undertaking the trial period. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmīti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’

Evañca pana, bhikkhave, chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ— And he should be given the trial period of six days in this way:

tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā … pe … The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … ‘Venerables, I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. … sohaṃ mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While undertaking the trial period, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, committed while undertaking the trial period, Taṃ maṃ saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. and the Order sent me back to the beginning. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmī’ti. I now ask the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, committed while undertaking the trial period.’

Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu … pe … This monk Udāyī … chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. is asking the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, committed while undertaking the trial period. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him the trial period of six days. Esā ñatti … pe … This is the motion. …

Dinnaṃ saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. The Order has given the monk Udāyī the trial period of six days for one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen, committed while undertaking the trial period. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.11. Abbhānārahamūlāyapaṭikassanā Sending back to the beginning of those deserving rehabilitation

So ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. When he had completed the trial period, while deserving rehabilitation, he committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. … sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. When I had completed the trial period, while deserving rehabilitation, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassitvā chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should send the monk Udāyī back to the beginning for one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen, committed while deserving rehabilitation. It should then give him the trial period of six days. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo … pe …. And he should be sent back to the beginning in this way: …

Evañca pana, bhikkhave, chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ … pe …. And he should be given the trial period of six days in this way: …

Dinnaṃ saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. The Order has given the monk Udāyī the trial period of six days for one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen, committed while deserving rehabilitation. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.12. Mūlāyapaṭikassitaabbhāna Rehabilitation of those sent back to the beginning

So ciṇṇamānatto bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— When he had completed the trial period, he told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. … sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto. I have now completed the trial period. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbhetu. “Well then, the Order should rehabilitate the monk Udāyī. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, abbhetabbo— And it should be done in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. ‘Venerables, I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for five days for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While on probation, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, Taṃ maṃ saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. When I had completed the probation, while deserving the trial period, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, Taṃ maṃ saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. When I had completed the probation, I asked the Order for the trial period of six days for the three offenses, Tassa me saṃgho tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me the trial period. Sohaṃ mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While undertaking the trial period, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, Taṃ maṃ saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. I then asked the Order to give me the trial period for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. which it did. Sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. When I had completed the trial period, while deserving rehabilitation, I committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, Taṃ maṃ saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. I then asked the Order to give me the trial period for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. which it gave me. Sohaṃ, bhante, ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācāmī’ti. I have now completed the trial period and I ask the Order for rehabilitation.’

Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for probation for five days for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya pañcāhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While he was on probation, he committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. He asked the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. So parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. When he had completed the probation, while deserving the trial period, he committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. He asked the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. So parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. When he had completed the probation, he asked the Order for the trial period of six days for the three offenses, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him the trial period. So mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. While he was undertaking the trial period, he committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. He asked the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. He then asked the Order to give him the trial period for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him the trial period. So ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ appaṭicchannaṃ. When he had completed the trial period, while deserving rehabilitation, he committed one unconcealed offense of intentional emission of semen. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. He asked the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. He then asked the Order to give him the trial period for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā appaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him the trial period. So ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. He has now completed the trial period and is asking the Order for rehabilitation. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should rehabilitate him. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. … so ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. He has now completed the trial period and is asking the Order for rehabilitation. Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheti. The Order rehabilitates him. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno abbhānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of rehabilitating him should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Abbhito saṃghena udāyī bhikkhu. The Order has rehabilitated the monk Udāyī. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.13. Pakkhappaṭicchannaparivāsa Probation for those with offenses concealed for a half-month

Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā udāyī ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpanno hoti sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. On one occasion Venerable Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks about this, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? adding, “What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should give the monk Udāyī probation for a half-month for one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo— And it should be given in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. ‘Venerables, I have committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. I ask the Order for probation for a half-month for that offense.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbo. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbo. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for probation for a half-month for that offense. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him that probation. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī has committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for probation for a half-month for that offense. Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ deti. The Order gives him that probation. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him that probation should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Dinno saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāso. The Order has given the monk Udāyī probation for a half-month for one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.14. Pakkhapārivāsikamūlāyapaṭikassana Sending back to the beginning for those on probation for a half-month

So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While he was on probation, he committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for a half-month for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While on probation, I committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti. What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassitvā purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should send the monk Udāyī back to the beginning for one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days and committed while on probation, and it should then give him probation simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo— And he should be sent back to the beginning in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. ‘Venerables, I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for a half-month for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While on probation, I committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācāmī’ti. I ask the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbā. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbā. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for probation for a half-month for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While he was on probation, he committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. He is now asking the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikasseyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should send him back to the beginning for that offense. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for probation for a half-month for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While he was on probation, he committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yācati. He is now asking the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense. Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassati. The Order sends him back to the beginning for that offense. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of sending him back to the beginning for that offense should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Paṭikassito saṃghena udāyī bhikkhu antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanā. The Order has sent the monk Udāyī back to the beginning for one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days and committed while on probation. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.15. Samodhānaparivāsa Simultaneous probations

“Evañca pana, bhikkhave, purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso dātabbo— “And he should be given probation simultaneous with probation for the previous offense in this way:

tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. ‘I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for a half-month for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While on probation, I committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, Taṃ maṃ saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. and the Order sent me back to the beginning. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. I now ask the Order for probation for that offense, simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense.’
