Dutiyampi yācitabbo. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbo. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for probation for a half-month for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While he was on probation, he committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. He asked the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. and the Order sent him back to the beginning. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is now asking the Order for probation for that offense, simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him that simultaneous probation. Esā ñatti. This is the motion. …

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for probation for a half-month for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While he was on probation, he committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. He asked the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. and the Order sent him back to the beginning. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is now asking the Order for probation for that offense, simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense. Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ deti. The Order gives him that simultaneous probation. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him that simultaneous probation should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Dinno saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso. The Order has given the monk Udāyī probation for one offense of intentional emission of semen—concealed for five days and committed while on probation—simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.16. Mānattārahamūlāyapaṭikassanādi Sending back to the beginning for those deserving the trial period, etc.

So parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. When he had completed the probation, while deserving the trial period, he committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. … sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. When I had completed the probation, while deserving the trial period, I committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassitvā purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should send the monk Udāyī back to the beginning for one offense of intentional emission of semen—concealed for five days and committed while deserving the trial period—and it should then give him probation simultaneous with probation for the previous offense. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo … pe …. And he should be sent back to the beginning in this way:

Evañca pana, bhikkhave, purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso dātabbo … pe … And he should be given probation simultaneous with probation for the previous offense in this way: …

deti … pe ….

Dinno saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso. The Order has given the monk Udāyī probation for one offense of intentional emission of semen—concealed for five days and committed while deserving the trial period—simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.17. Tikāpattimānatta Trial period for the three offenses

So parivutthaparivāso bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— When he had completed the probation, he told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month … sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso. I have now completed the probation. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should give the monk Udāyī the trial period of six days for the three offenses. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbaṃ— And it should be given in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … ‘Venerables, I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. … sohaṃ, bhante, parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācāmī’ti. I have now completed that probation and I ask the Order for the trial period of six days for the three offenses.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. … so parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. He has now completed that probation and is asking the Order for the trial period of six days for the three offenses. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him the trial period of six days for the three offenses. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. … so parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yācati. He has now completed that probation and is asking the Order for the trial period of six days for the three offenses. Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ deti. The Order gives him the trial period of six days for the three offenses. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him the trial period of six days for the three offenses should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Dinnaṃ saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. The Order has given the monk Udāyī the trial period of six days for the three offenses. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.18. Mānattacārikamūlāyapaṭikassanādi Sending back to the beginning of those undertaking the trial period, etc.

So mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While he was undertaking the trial period, he committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. … sohaṃ mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While undertaking the trial period, I committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassitvā purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ datvā chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should send the monk Udāyī back to the beginning for one offense of intentional emission of semen—concealed for five days and committed while undertaking the trial period—and it should then give him probation for that offense simultaneous with probation for the previous offense, and it should then give him the trial period of six days. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo … pe …. And he should be sent back to the beginning in this way: …

Evañca pana, bhikkhave, purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso dātabbo … pe …. And he should be given probation simultaneous with probation for the previous offense in this way: …

Evañca pana, bhikkhave, chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ … pe … And he should be given the trial period of six days in this way: …

deti … pe ….

Dinnaṃ saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. The Order has given the monk Udāyī the trial period of six days for one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days and committed while undertaking the trial period. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.19. Abbhānārahamūlāyapaṭikassanādi Sending back to the beginning of those deserving rehabilitation, etc.

So ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. When he had completed the trial period, while deserving rehabilitation, he committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. … sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. When I had completed the trial period, while deserving rehabilitation, I committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassitvā purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ datvā chārattaṃ mānattaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should send the monk Udāyī back to the beginning for one offense of intentional emission of semen—concealed for five days and committed while deserving rehabilitation—and it should then give him probation for that offense simultaneous with probation for the previous offense, and it should then give him the trial period of six days. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, mūlāya paṭikassitabbo … pe …. And he should be sent back to the beginning in this way: …

Evañca pana, bhikkhave, purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāso dātabbo … pe …. And he should be given probation simultaneous with probation for the previous offense in this way: …

Evañca pana, bhikkhave, chārattaṃ mānattaṃ dātabbaṃ … pe … And he should be given the trial period of six days in this way: …

deti … pe ….

Dinnaṃ saṃghena udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ. The Order has given the monk Udāyī the trial period of six days for one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days and committed while deserving rehabilitation. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

1.20. Pakkhappaṭicchannaabbhāna Rehabilitation of those with offenses concealed for a half-month

So ciṇṇamānatto bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— When he had completed the trial period, he told the monks, “ahaṃ, āvuso, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … “I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. … sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto. I have now completed the trial period. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbhetu. “Well then, the Order should rehabilitate the monk Udāyī. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, abbhetabbo— And it should be done in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, udāyinā bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā, ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā, vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā, ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā, añjaliṃ paggahetvā, evamassa vacanīyo— The monk Udāyī should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. ‘Venerables, I had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order for probation for a half-month for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Sohaṃ parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While on probation, I committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, Taṃ maṃ saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I then asked the Order to give me probation for that offense, simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense, Tassa me saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that simultaneous probation. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. When I had completed the probation, while deserving the trial period of six days, I committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, Taṃ maṃ saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I then asked the Order to give me probation for that offense, simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense, Tassa me saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that simultaneous probation. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. When I had completed the probation, I asked the Order for the trial period of six days for the three offenses, Tassa me saṃgho tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me the trial period. Sohaṃ mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While undertaking the trial period, I committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, Taṃ maṃ saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I then asked the Order to give me probation for that offense, simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense, Tassa me saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that simultaneous probation. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. When I had completed the probation, I asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me the trial period. Sohaṃ ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajjiṃ sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. When I had completed the trial period, while deserving rehabilitation, I committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāciṃ. I asked the Order to send me back to the beginning for that offense, Taṃ maṃ saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I then asked the Order to give me probation for that offense, simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense, Tassa me saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that simultaneous probation. Sohaṃ parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāciṃ. When I had completed the probation, I asked the Order for the trial period of six days for that offense, Tassa me saṃgho antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me the trial period. Sohaṃ, bhante, ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācāmī’ti. I have now completed the trial period and I ask the Order for rehabilitation.’

Dutiyampi yācitabbaṃ. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbaṃ. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ. This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ yāci. He asked the Order for probation for a half-month for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pakkhappaṭicchannāya pakkhaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. So parivasanto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While he was on probation, he committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. He asked the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāci. He then asked the Order to give him probation for that offense, simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that simultaneous probation. So parivutthaparivāso mānattāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. When he had completed the probation, while deserving the trial period of six days, he committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. He asked the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāci. He then asked the Order to give him probation for that offense, simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that simultaneous probation. So parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. When he had completed the probation, he asked the Order for the trial period of six days for the three offenses, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno tissannaṃ āpattīnaṃ chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him the trial period. So mānattaṃ caranto antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. While he was undertaking the trial period, he committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. He asked the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāci. He then asked the Order to give him probation for that offense, simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that simultaneous probation. So parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. He then asked the Order to give him the trial period of six days for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him the trial period. So ciṇṇamānatto abbhānāraho antarā ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pañcāhappaṭicchannaṃ. When he had completed the trial period, while deserving rehabilitation, he committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for five days. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāyapaṭikassanaṃ yāci. He asked the Order to send him back to the beginning for that offense, Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya mūlāya paṭikassi. which it did. So saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ yāci. He then asked the Order to give him probation for that offense, simultaneous with the probation for the previous offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya purimāya āpattiyā samodhānaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that simultaneous probation. So parivutthaparivāso saṃghaṃ antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ yāci. When he had completed the probation, he asked the Order to give him the trial period of six days for that offense, Saṃgho udāyissa bhikkhuno antarā ekissā āpattiyā sañcetanikāya sukkavissaṭṭhiyā pañcāhappaṭicchannāya chārattaṃ mānattaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him the trial period. So ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. He has now completed the trial period and is asking the Order for rehabilitation. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should rehabilitate him. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ udāyī bhikkhu ekaṃ āpattiṃ āpajji sañcetanikaṃ sukkavissaṭṭhiṃ pakkhappaṭicchannaṃ … pe … This monk Udāyī had committed one offense of intentional emission of semen, concealed for a half-month. … so ciṇṇamānatto saṃghaṃ abbhānaṃ yācati. He has now completed the trial period and is asking the Order for rehabilitation. Saṃgho udāyiṃ bhikkhuṃ abbheti. The Order rehabilitates him. Yassāyasmato khamati udāyissa bhikkhuno abbhānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of rehabilitating him should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Abbhito saṃghena udāyī bhikkhu. The Order has rehabilitated the monk Udāyī. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

Sukkavissaṭṭhi samattā. The section on emission of semen is finished.

2. 2 Parivāsa Probation

2.1. Agghasamodhānaparivāsa Simultaneous probations according to the longest duration

Tena kho pana samayena aññataro bhikkhu sambahulā saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpanno hoti— At one time a monk had committed many offenses entailing suspension: ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti dvīhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti tīhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti catūhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti pañcāhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti chāhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti sattāhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti aṭṭhāhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti navāhappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā. one concealed for one day, one for two days, one for three days, one for four days, one for five days, one for six days, one for seven days, one for eight days, one for nine days, and one for ten days. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks about this, “ahaṃ, āvuso, sambahulā saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ— ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā … pe … ekā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? adding, “What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho tassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should give that monk simultaneous probation according to the longest duration, that is, for the offense that was concealed for ten days. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo— And it should be given in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … That monk should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, sambahulā saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ— ‘Venerables, I have committed many offenses entailing suspension: ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā … pe … one concealed for one day … ekā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā. one for ten days. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. I ask the Order for simultaneous probation according to the longest duration, that is, for the offense that was concealed for ten days.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbo. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbo. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu sambahulā saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji— This monk so-and-so has committed many offenses entailing suspension: ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā … pe … one concealed for one day … ekā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā. one for ten days. So saṃghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for simultaneous probation according to the longest duration, that is, for the offense that was concealed for ten days. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him that simultaneous probation. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu sambahulā saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji— This monk so-and-so has committed many offenses entailing suspension: ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā … pe … one concealed for one day … ekā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā. one for ten days. So saṃghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for simultaneous probation according to the longest duration, that is, for the offense that was concealed for ten days. Saṃgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ deti. The Order gives him that simultaneous probation. Yassāyasmato khamati itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā; Any monk who approves of giving him that simultaneous probation tassā agghena samodhānaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Dinno saṃghena itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpatti dasāhappaṭicchannā tassā agghena samodhānaparivāso. The Order has given monk so-and-so simultaneous probation according to the longest duration, that is, for the offense that was concealed for ten days. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

2.2. Sabbacirappaṭicchannaagghasamodhāna Simultaneous probations according to the longest duration, that is, for all the offenses that were concealed the longest

Tena kho pana samayena aññataro bhikkhu sambahulā saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpanno hoti— At one time a monk had committed many offenses entailing suspension: ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā, dve āpattiyo dvīhappaṭicchannāyo, tisso āpattiyo tīhappaṭicchannāyo, catasso āpattiyo catūhappaṭicchannāyo, pañca āpattiyo pañcāhappaṭicchannāyo, cha āpattiyo chāhappaṭicchannāyo, satta āpattiyo sattāhappaṭicchannāyo, aṭṭha āpattiyo aṭṭhāhappaṭicchannāyo, nava āpattiyo navāhappaṭicchannāyo, dasa āpattiyo dasāhappaṭicchannāyo. one concealed for one day, two for two days, three for three days, four for four days, five for five days, six for six days, seven for seven days, eight for eight days, nine for nine days, ten for ten days. So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks about this, “ahaṃ, āvuso, sambahulā saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ, ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā … pe … dasa āpattiyo dasāhappaṭicchannāyo. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? adding, “What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho tassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should give that monk simultaneous probation according to the longest duration, that is, for all the offenses that were concealed the longest. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo— And it should be given in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … That monk should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, sambahulā saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ, ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā … pe … ‘Venerables, I have committed many offenses entailing suspension: one concealed for one day … dasa āpattiyo dasāhappaṭicchannāyo. ten for ten days. Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. I ask the Order for simultaneous probation according to the longest duration, that is, for all the offenses that were concealed the longest.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbo. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbo. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu sambahulā saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji, ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā … pe … This monk so-and-so has committed many offenses entailing suspension: one concealed for one day … dasa āpattiyo dasāhappaṭicchannāyo. ten for ten days. So saṃghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for simultaneous probation according to the longest duration, that is, for all the offenses that were concealed the longest. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ saṃgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him that simultaneous probation. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu sambahulā saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji— This monk so-and-so has committed many offenses entailing suspension: ekā āpatti ekāhappaṭicchannā … pe … one concealed for one day … dasa āpattiyo dasāhappaṭicchannāyo. ten for ten days. So saṃghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is asking the Order for simultaneous probation according to the longest duration, that is, for all the offenses that were concealed the longest. Saṃgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsaṃ deti. The Order gives him that simultaneous probation. Yassāyasmato khamati itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him that simultaneous probation should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Dinno saṃghena itthannāmassa bhikkhuno tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ yā āpattiyo sabbacirappaṭicchannāyo tāsaṃ agghena samodhānaparivāso. The Order has given monk so-and-so simultaneous probation according to the longest duration, that is, for all the offenses that were concealed the longest. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’”ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’”

2.3. Dvemāsaparivāsa Probation for two months

Tena kho pana samayena aññataro bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpanno hoti dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. At one time a monk had committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Tassa etadahosi— He thought, “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. “I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for one of those offenses.” So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāci. He did, Tassa saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. Tassa parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— While he was on probation, he was conscience-stricken. “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. He considered what he had done, Tassa me etadahosi— ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— ‘yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan’”ti. and then thought, “Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for the other offense too.”

So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks everything that had happened, “ahaṃ, āvuso, dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa me etadahosi— ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa me etadahosi— “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”’ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— ‘yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? adding, “What should I do now?” Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho tassa bhikkhuno itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should give that monk probation for two months for that offense. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo— And it should be given in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā, ekaṃsaṃ uttarāsaṅgaṃ karitvā, vuḍḍhānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ pāde vanditvā, ukkuṭikaṃ nisīditvā, añjaliṃ paggahetvā, evamassa vacanīyo— That monk should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. ‘Venerables, I had committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Tassa me etadahosi— I thought, “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. “I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for one of those offenses.” Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I did, Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— While on probation, I was conscience-stricken. “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. I considered what I had done, Tassa me etadahosi— ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— “yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. and then thought, “Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for the other offense too.” Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. And now I ask the Order for probation for two months for the other offense, concealed for two months.’

Dutiyampi yācitabbo. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbo. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Venerables, let the Order listen to me. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. This monk so-and-so had committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Tassa etadahosi— He thought, “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. “I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for one of those offenses.” So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāci. He did, Tassa saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. Tassa parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— While he was on probation, he was conscience-stricken. “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. He considered what he had done, Tassa me etadahosi— ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— “yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. and then thought, “Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for the other offense too.” So saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is now asking the Order for probation for two months for that other offense. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him probation for two months for that other offense. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. This monk so-and-so had committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Tassa etadahosi— He thought, “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. “I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for one of those offenses.” So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāci. He did, Tassa saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. Tassa parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— While he was on probation, he was conscience-stricken. “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. He considered what he had done, Tassa me etadahosi— ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— “yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. and then thought, “Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for the other offense too.” So saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He is now asking the Order for probation for two months for that other offense. Saṃgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. The Order gives him probation for two months for that other offense. Yassāyasmato khamati itthannāmassa bhikkhuno itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him probation for two months for that other offense should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Dinno saṃghena itthannāmassa bhikkhuno itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāso. The Order has given monk so-and-so probation for two months for the other offense, concealed for two months. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’

Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā tadupādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā. Starting right there, that monk must stay on probation for two months.”

2.4. Dvemāsāparivasitabbavidhi Processes for staying on probation for two months

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. “It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Tassa evaṃ hoti— He thinks, ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. ‘I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for one of those offenses.’ So saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He does, Tassa saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. Tassa parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— While on probation, he is conscience-stricken. ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. He considers all this Tassa me etadahosi— “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho ekissā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— “yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”’ti. and thinks, ‘Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for the other offense too.’ So saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He then asks the Order, Tassa saṃgho itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him probation for two months for the other offense too. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā tadupādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā. Starting right there, that monk must stay on probation for two months.

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. ekaṃ āpattiṃ jānāti, ekaṃ āpattiṃ na jānāti. He knows about one offense, but not about the other. So saṃghaṃ yaṃ āpattiṃ jānāti, tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He asks the Order for probation for two months for the offense he knows about, Tassa saṃgho tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. So parivasanto itarampi āpattiṃ jānāti. While on probation, he finds out about the other offense. Tassa evaṃ hoti— He considers all this ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekaṃ āpattiṃ jāniṃ, ekaṃ āpattiṃ na jāniṃ. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ yaṃ āpattiṃ jāniṃ tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto itarampi āpattiṃ jānāmi. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. and thinks, ‘Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for the other offense too.’ So saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He then asks the Order, Tassa saṃgho itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him probation for two months for the other offense too. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā tadupādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā. Starting right there, that monk must stay on probation for two months.

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. ekaṃ āpattiṃ sarati, ekaṃ āpattiṃ nassarati. He remembers one offense, but not the other. So saṃghaṃ yaṃ āpattiṃ sarati, tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He asks the Order for probation for two months for the offense he remembers, Tassa saṃgho tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. So parivasanto itarampi āpattiṃ sarati. While on probation, he remembers the other offense. Tassa evaṃ hoti— He considers all this ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekaṃ āpattiṃ sariṃ, ekaṃ āpattiṃ nassariṃ. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ yaṃ āpattiṃ sariṃ, tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto itarampi āpattiṃ sarāmi. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. and thinks, ‘Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for the other offense too.’ So saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He then asks the Order, Tassa saṃgho itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him probation for two months for the other offense too. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā tadupādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā. Starting right there, that monk must stay on probation for two months.

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. ekāya āpattiyā nibbematiko, ekāya āpattiyā vematiko. He is certain that one is an offense, but has doubts about the other. So saṃghaṃ yāya āpattiyā nibbematiko, tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He asks the Order for probation for two months for the offense he is certain about, Tassa saṃgho tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. So parivasanto itarissāpi āpattiyā nibbematiko hoti. While on probation, he becomes certain that the other is an offense too. Tassa evaṃ hoti— He considers all this ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekāya āpattiyā nibbematiko, ekāya āpattiyā vematiko. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ yāya āpattiyā nibbematiko tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho tassā āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto itarissāpi āpattiyā nibbematiko. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. and thinks, ‘Let me ask the Order for probation for two months for the other offense too.’ So saṃghaṃ itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He then asks the Order, Tassa saṃgho itarissāpi āpattiyā dvemāsappaṭicchannāya dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him probation for two months for the other offense too. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā tadupādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā. Starting right there, that monk must stay on probation for two months.

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; “It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. ekā āpatti jānappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti ajānappaṭicchannā. He concealed one offense knowingly, but the other unknowingly. So saṃghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He asks the Order for probation for two months for both offenses, Tassa saṃgho tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. Tassa parivasantassa añño bhikkhu āgacchati bahussuto āgatāgamo dhammadharo vinayadharo mātikādharo paṇḍito viyatto medhāvī lajjī kukkuccako sikkhākāmo. While he is on probation, another monk arrives. He is learned, a master of the tradition; he is an expert on the Teaching, the Monastic Law, and the summaries; he is wise and competent, has sense of conscience, and is afraid of wrongdoing and fond of the training. So evaṃ vadeti— He says, ‘kiṃ ayaṃ, āvuso, bhikkhu āpanno? ‘What has this monk committed? Kissāyaṃ bhikkhu parivasatī’ti? Why is he on probation?’ Te evaṃ vadenti— They tell him everything, ‘ayaṃ, āvuso, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekā āpatti jānappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti ajānappaṭicchannā. So saṃghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. Tassa saṃgho tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tāyo ayaṃ, āvuso, bhikkhu āpanno, tāsāyaṃ bhikkhu parivasatī’ti. So evaṃ vadeti— and he says, ‘yāyaṃ, āvuso, āpatti jānappaṭicchannā, dhammikaṃ tassā āpattiyā parivāsadānaṃ; ‘The giving of probation for the offense concealed knowingly is legitimate, dhammattā ruhati. legal, and has effect. Yā ca khvāyaṃ, āvuso, āpatti ajānappaṭicchannā, adhammikaṃ tassā āpattiyā parivāsadānaṃ; The giving of probation for the offense concealed unknowingly is illegitimate, adhammattā na ruhati. illegal, and has no effect. Ekissā, āvuso, āpattiyā bhikkhu mānattāraho’ti. He deserves the trial period for the one offense only.’

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. ekā āpatti saramānappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti assaramānappaṭicchannā. He concealed one offense while remembering it, but the other without remembering it. So saṃghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He asks the Order for probation for two months for both offenses, Tassa saṃgho tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. So saṃghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāci. Tassa saṃgho tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Ekissā, āvuso, āpattiyā bhikkhu mānattāraho’ti. He deserves the trial period for the one offense only.’

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. ekā āpatti nibbematikappaṭicchannā, ekā āpatti vematikappaṭicchannā. He concealed one offense while having no doubts about it, but the other while having doubts about it. So saṃghaṃ tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He asks the Order for probation for two months for both offenses, Tassa saṃgho tāsaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. Ekissā, āvuso, āpattiyā bhikkhu mānattāraho’”ti. He deserves the trial period for the one offense only.’”

Tena kho pana samayena aññataro bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpanno hoti dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. At one time a monk committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Tassa etadahosi— He thought, “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. ‘I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Let me ask the Order for probation for one month for those offenses.’ So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāci. He did, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. Tassa parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— While he was on probation, he was conscience-stricken. “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. He considered all this, Tassa me etadahosi— ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. and then thought, ‘Let me ask the Order for probation for an additional month for those two offenses.’

So bhikkhūnaṃ ārocesi— He told the monks about everything, “ahaṃ kho, āvuso, dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa me etadahosi— ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Tassa me etadahosi— “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”’ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— ‘yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. Kathaṃ nu kho mayā paṭipajjitabban”ti? adding, ‘What should I do now?’ Bhagavato etamatthaṃ ārocesuṃ. They told the Master and he said:

“Tena hi, bhikkhave, saṃgho tassa bhikkhuno dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ detu. “Well then, the Order should give that monk probation for an additional month for those two offenses concealed for two months. Evañca pana, bhikkhave, dātabbo— And it should be given in this way:

Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā saṃghaṃ upasaṅkamitvā … pe … That monk should approach the Order, put his upper robe over one shoulder, pay respect at the feet of the senior monks, squat on his heels, put the palms of his hands together, evamassa vacanīyo— and say:

‘ahaṃ, bhante, dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. ‘Venerables, I had committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Tassa me etadahosi— I thought, “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. ‘I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Let me ask the Order for probation for one month for those offenses.’ Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. I did, Tassa me saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave me that probation. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— While on probation, I was conscience-stricken. “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. I considered all this, Tassa me etadahosi— ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— “yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. and then thought, ‘Let me ask the Order for probation for an additional month for those two offenses.’ Sohaṃ, bhante, saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yācāmī’ti. I now ask the Order for probation for an additional month for those two offenses.’ Dutiyampi yācitabbo. And he should ask a second Tatiyampi yācitabbo. and a third time. Byattena bhikkhunā paṭibalena saṃgho ñāpetabbo— A competent and capable monk should then inform the Order:

‘Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. ‘Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. This monk so-and-so had committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Tassa etadahosi— He thought, “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. ‘I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Let me ask the Order for probation for one month for those offenses.’ So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāci. He did, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. Tassa parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— While he was on probation, he was conscience-stricken. “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. He considered all this, Tassa me etadahosi— ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo— “yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami. “Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. and then thought, ‘Let me ask the Order for probation for an additional month for those two offenses.’ So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yācati. He is now asking the Order for probation for an additional month for those two offenses. Yadi saṃghassa pattakallaṃ, saṃgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ dadeyya. If it seems appropriate to the Order, the Order should give him that probation. Esā ñatti. This is the motion.

Suṇātu me, bhante, saṃgho. Please, Venerables, I ask the Order to listen. Ayaṃ itthannāmo bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. This monk so-and-so had committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Tassa etadahosi— He thought, “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Let me ask the Order for probation for one month for those offenses.’ So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāci. He did, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. and the Order gave him that probation. Tassa parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— While he was on probation, he was conscience-stricken. “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. He considered all this, Tassa me etadahosi— ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— “yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. and then thought, ‘Let me ask the Order for probation for an additional month for those two offenses.’ So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yācati. He is now asking the Order for probation for an additional month for those two offenses. Saṃgho itthannāmassa bhikkhuno dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ deti. The Order gives him that probation. Yassāyasmato khamati itthannāmassa bhikkhuno dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsassa dānaṃ, so tuṇhassa; Any monk who approves of giving him that probation should remain silent. yassa nakkhamati, so bhāseyya. Any monk who does not approve should speak up.

Dutiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe … For the second time I speak on this matter. … tatiyampi etamatthaṃ vadāmi … pe …. For the third time I speak on this matter. …

Dinno saṃghena itthannāmassa bhikkhuno dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāso. The Order has given monk so-and-so probation for an additional month for those two offenses, concealed for two months. Khamati saṃghassa, tasmā tuṇhī, evametaṃ dhārayāmī’ti. The Order approves and is therefore silent. I will remember it thus.’

Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā purimaṃ upādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā. When the previous month is included, that monk must stay on probation for two months.

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. “It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Tassa evaṃ hoti— He thinks, ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. ‘I have committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. Let me ask the Order for probation for one month for those offenses.’ So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He does, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. Tassa parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— While on probation, he is conscience-stricken. ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. He considers all this Tassa me etadahosi— “ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ ekamāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tassa me parivasantassa lajjīdhammo okkami— “Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yāceyyan”ti. and thinks, ‘Let me ask the Order for probation for an additional month for those two offenses.’ So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yācati. He then asks the Order, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him probation for an additional month. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā purimaṃ upādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā. When the previous month is included, that monk must stay on probation for two months.

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. ekaṃ māsaṃ jānāti, ekaṃ māsaṃ na jānāti. He knows about one month, but not the other. So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ yaṃ māsaṃ jānāti taṃ māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yācati. He asks the Order for one month probation for the month he knows about, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ yaṃ māsaṃ jānāti taṃ māsaṃ parivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. So parivasanto itarampi māsaṃ jānāti. While on probation, he finds out about the other month. Tassa evaṃ hoti— He considers all of this ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekaṃ māsaṃ jāniṃ, ekaṃ māsaṃ na jāniṃ. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ yaṃ māsaṃ jāniṃ taṃ māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ yaṃ māsaṃ jāniṃ taṃ māsaṃ parivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto itarampi māsaṃ jānāmi. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. and thinks, ‘Let me ask the Order for probation for an additional month for those two offenses.’ So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yācati. He then asks the Order, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him probation for an additional month. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā purimaṃ upādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā. When the previous month is included, that monk must stay on probation for two months.

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. ekaṃ māsaṃ sarati, ekaṃ māsaṃ nassarati. He remembers one month, but not the other. So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ yaṃ māsaṃ sarati taṃ māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yācati. He asks the Order for one month probation for the month he remembers, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ yaṃ māsaṃ sarati taṃ māsaṃ parivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. So parivasanto itarampi māsaṃ sarati. While on probation, he remembers the other month. Tassa evaṃ hoti— He considers all of this ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekaṃ māsaṃ sariṃ, ekaṃ māsaṃ nassariṃ. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ yaṃ māsaṃ sariṃ taṃ māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ yaṃ māsaṃ sariṃ taṃ māsaṃ parivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto itarampi māsaṃ sarāmi. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. and thinks, ‘Let me ask the Order for probation for an additional month for those two offenses.’ So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yācati. He then asks the Order, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him probation for an additional month. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā purimaṃ upādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā. When the previous month is included, that monk must stay on probation for two months.

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. ekaṃ māsaṃ nibbematiko, ekaṃ māsaṃ vematiko. He is certain about one month, but has doubts about the other. So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ yaṃ māsaṃ nibbematiko taṃ māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yācati. He asks the Order for one month probation for the month he is certain about, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ yaṃ māsaṃ nibbematiko taṃ māsaṃ parivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. So parivasanto itarampi māsaṃ nibbematiko hoti. While on probation, he becomes certain about the other month. Tassa evaṃ hoti— He considers all this ‘ahaṃ kho dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjiṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; ekaṃ māsaṃ nibbematiko, ekaṃ māsaṃ vematiko. Sohaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ yaṃ māsaṃ nibbematiko taṃ māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yāciṃ. Tassa me saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchānnānaṃ yaṃ māsaṃ nibbematiko taṃ māsaṃ parivāsaṃ adāsi. Sohaṃ parivasanto itarampi māsaṃ nibbematiko. Yannūnāhaṃ saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yāceyyan’ti. and thinks, ‘Let me ask the Order for probation for an additional month for those two offenses.’ So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ yācati. He then asks the Order, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ itarampi māsaṃ parivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him probation for an additional month. Tena, bhikkhave, bhikkhunā purimaṃ upādāya dve māsā parivasitabbā. When the previous month is included, that monk must stay on probation for two months.

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; “It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. eko māso jānappaṭicchanno, eko māso ajānappaṭicchanno. He concealed one month knowingly, but the other unknowingly. So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He asks the Order for probation for two months for both offenses, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. Tassa parivasantassa añño bhikkhu āgacchati bahussuto āgatāgamo dhammadharo vinayadharo mātikādharo paṇḍito viyatto medhāvī lajjī kukkuccako sikkhākāmo. While he is on probation, another monk arrives. He is learned, a master of the tradition; he is an expert on the Teaching, the Monastic Law, and the summaries; he is wise and competent, has sense of conscience, and is afraid of wrongdoing and fond of the training. So evaṃ vadeti— He says, ‘kiṃ ayaṃ, āvuso, bhikkhu āpanno? ‘What has this monk committed? Kissāyaṃ bhikkhu parivasatī’ti? Why is he on probation?’ Te evaṃ vadenti— They tell him everything, ‘ayaṃ, āvuso, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajji dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo. Eko māso jānappaṭicchanno, eko māso ajānappaṭicchanno. So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yāci. Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ adāsi. Tāyo ayaṃ, āvuso, bhikkhu āpanno tāsāyaṃ bhikkhu parivasatī’ti. So evaṃ vadeti— and he says, ‘yvāyaṃ, āvuso, māso jānappaṭicchanno dhammikaṃ tassa māsassa parivāsadānaṃ; ‘The giving of probation for the month concealed knowingly is legitimate, dhammattā ruhati. legal, and has effect. Yo ca khvāyaṃ, āvuso, māso ajānappaṭicchanno adhammikaṃ tassa māsassa parivāsadānaṃ; The giving of probation for the month concealed unknowingly is illegitimate, adhammattā na ruhati. illegal, and has no effect. Ekassa, āvuso, māsassa bhikkhu mānattāraho’ti. He deserves the trial period only in relation to the one month.’

Idha pana, bhikkhave, bhikkhu dve saṃghādisesā āpattiyo āpajjati dvemāsappaṭicchannāyo; It may be that a monk has committed two offenses entailing suspension, both concealed for two months. eko māso saramānappaṭicchanno, eko māso assaramānappaṭicchanno. He concealed one month while remembering it, but the other without remembering it. So saṃghaṃ dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ yācati. He asks the Order for probation for two months for both offenses, Tassa saṃgho dvinnaṃ āpattīnaṃ dvemāsappaṭicchannānaṃ dvemāsaparivāsaṃ deti. and the Order gives him that probation. Tassa parivasantassa añño bhikkhu āgacchati bahussuto āgatāgamo dhammadharo vinayadharo mātikādharo paṇḍito viyatto medhāvī lajjī kukkuccako sikkhākāmo. While he is on probation, another monk arrives.
